49.21(1): gi sa chen non/ bswo A+o~M tshangs la gu dun gyer la g.yu 'brang spungs so ram bswo tha/
50.1(1): bswo oM tshangs la gu thun g.yu 'brang bdud rtsir bswo tha/ bswo A+o~M tshangs la gu thun 
50.2(1): gyer la g.yu 'brang spungs so khod do ram bswo tha/ bswo A+o~M tshangs la gu dun rta na h+phi 
50.3(1): phaT bswo tha/ bswo oM tshangs la gu thun gyer la g.yu 'brang spungs so li min tri bswo 
50.4(1): tha/ bswo A+o~M tshangs la gu thun 'ag+ha na h+phi phaT bswo tha/ bswo oM tshangs la gu thun gyer 
50.5(1): la g.yu 'brang spungs so mu ber sangs ste ram bswo tha/ bswo oM tshangs la gu thun pa 
50.6(1): na tri ram bswo tha/ bswo A+o~M tshangs la gu thun gyer la g.yu 'brang spungs so smar ro 
50.7(1): ram tri bswo tha/ bswo oM tshangs la gu thun mu ru spungs so ram bswo tha/ bdud rtsi 
50.8(1): sman gyi pho brang na/ gzungs thag btags te spyi bor bzung / bzlas brjod sngags

50.11(1): bskur/ e ma ho/ rigs lnga gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor du/ khro bo yab yum dbang

50.14(1): tshangs la gu thun sad min spungs 'bur khri phaT ram bswo tha/ bswo A+o~M tshangs pa'i 
50.15(1): g.yu 'brang bdud rtsir tri du da na raM bswo tha/ bswo oM tshangs la gu thun sad min 
50.16(1): spungs lag shan 'dri na phaT ram bswo tha/ bswo oM tshangs pa'i g.yu 'brang bdud

50.18(1): h+phi phaT ram bswo tha/ bswo A+o~M tshangs pa'i g.yu 'brang bdud rtsir sa na li phra ni ram 
50.19(1): bswo tha/ bswo A+o~M tshangs la gu thun sad min spungs na dan tra d+hi na phaT ram bswo tha/
50.20(1): bswo oM tshangs pa'i g.yu 'brang bdud rtsir sa na la pra ni raM bswo tha/ gzungs thag 
50.21(1): dpral ba'i thad kar bzung / 'phro 'du byin rlabs rdzogs par bskur/ gnyis med

51.5(1): tri na raM bswo tha/ bswo A+o~M tshangs la gu thun tri myag tri na ram bswo tha/ bswo A+o~M tshangs
